The frontend calls the AKS-hosted API. The API queries Azure SQL. Each hop is restricted by NSG rules — no tier can be reached by anything other than its intended upstream.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003chr\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eWhy Hub-and-Spoke?\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-why-hub-and-spoke\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Why Hub-and-Spoke?\" href=\"#why-hub-and-spoke\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe job description mentions Hub-and-Spoke as part of the platform architecture at TJIP. This pattern separates shared infrastructure (firewall, VPN gateways, DNS) in the Hub from workload resources in the Spoke. It is the standard approach in Azure landing zones and makes it easy to add more spokes (e.g. a staging spoke, a production spoke) without touching shared services.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eWhy AKS for the application tier?\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-why-aks-for-the-application-tier\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Why AKS for the application tier?\" href=\"#why-aks-for-the-application-tier\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAKS is listed as a core part of TJIP's tech stack. Using it here — instead of a second App Service — shows how the API tier would work in practice. I chose \u003cstrong\u003eAzure CNI\u003c/strong\u003e for networking because it assigns pod IPs directly from the AKS subnet, which means NSG rules and VNet peering work natively without overlay networks. The \u003ccode\u003e/23\u003c/code\u003e subnet gives AKS enough IP space to scale.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eWhy App Service for the web tier?\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-why-app-service-for-the-web-tier\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Why App Service for the web tier?\" href=\"#why-app-service-for-the-web-tier\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eA simple frontend does not need container orchestration. App Service is fully managed, supports VNet integration, and keeps the presentation tier lightweight. This also shows I can pick the right service for the job rather than using AKS for everything.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eInstead of deploying custom application code, the frontend runs \u003cstrong\u003eMicrosoft's official sample container\u003c/strong\u003e (\u003ccode\u003emcr.microsoft.com/appsvc/staticsite:latest\u003c/code\u003e). This is a public image from the Microsoft Container Registry designed exactly for infrastructure demos — it gives you a working web page that confirms the App Service is running correctly. In a real project, this would be swapped for the team's frontend container or code via CI/CD.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eWhy Azure SQL with VNet rules?\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-why-azure-sql-with-vnet-rules\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Why Azure SQL with VNet rules?\" href=\"#why-azure-sql-with-vnet-rules\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAzure SQL is a managed relational database — no patching, no backups to manage. I locked it down with \u003ccode\u003epublic_network_access_enabled = false\u003c/code\u003e and a VNet service endpoint rule so only the data subnet can reach it. In production I would use a Private Endpoint instead (more secure, but more complex for a demo).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eSecurity \u0026amp; compliance thinking\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-security--compliance-thinking\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Security \u0026amp; compliance thinking\" href=\"#security--compliance-thinking\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eEven though this is a small demo, I made choices that reflect an ISO27001/SOC2-aware mindset:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSystem-assigned Managed Identity\u003c/strong\u003e on AKS, avoids storing service principal secrets.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eNSG deny-all rules\u003c/strong\u003e on the app and data subnets — explicit deny at the bottom of the rule list.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSQL password as a sensitive variable\u003c/strong\u003e — Terraform will not show it in plan output.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePublic access disabled\u003c/strong\u003e on the SQL server.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eConsistent tagging\u003c/strong\u003e — every resource gets \u003ccode\u003eProject\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eEnvironment\u003c/code\u003e, and \u003ccode\u003eManagedBy\u003c/code\u003e tags for audit trails.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eWhat I intentionally left focused:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cmarkdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\u003ctable\u003e\n\u003cthead\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eExcluded\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eWhy it matters in production\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/thead\u003e\n\u003ctbody\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eAzure Firewall resource\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eThe Hub subnet is ready for it, but the firewall SKU is expensive for a demo\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eIngress controller (NGINX / App Gateway)\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eNeeded to route external traffic into AKS pods\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eAzure Monitor + Grafana\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eTJIP's observability stack — out of scope per the assignment\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eAzure DevOps CI/CD pipelines\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eOut of scope per the assignment\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eTerragrunt wrapper\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eWould use in production for DRY config across environments\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eRemote state backend\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eWould use Azure Storage Account with blob lease locking\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eKey Vault for secrets\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eSQL password would live here instead of in a variable\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003ePrivate Endpoints\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003eMore secure than VNet rules, but adds Azure 3-Tier Application Infrastructure","","A Terraform project that defines infrastructure for a 3-tier web application on Microsoft Azure, using a **Hub-and-Spoke network topology** — the same pattern used in landing zones for financial-sector platforms.","","No application code is deployed. This is purely infrastructure-as-code.","","---","","## Architecture overview","","```","                    ┌──────────────────────────────────────┐","                    │        Hub VNet  10.0.0.0/16         │","                    │                                      │","                    │   ┌──────────────────────────────┐   │","                    │   │  AzureFirewallSubnet          │   │","                    │   │  10.0.1.0/24                  │   │","                    │   │  (central egress \u0026 logging)   │   │","                    │   └──────────────────────────────┘   │","                    └──────────────┬───────────────────────┘","                                   │","                              VNet Peering","                                   │","┌──────────────────────────────────┴───────────────────────────────────┐","│                     Spoke VNet  10.1.0.0/16                         │","│                                                                     │","│  ┌─────────────────┐  ┌─────────────────┐  ┌─────────────────┐     │","│  │  TIER 1 · WEB   │  │  TIER 2 · APP   │  │  TIER 3 · DATA  │     │","│  │                 │  │                 │  │                 │     │","│  │  App Service    │  │  AKS Cluster    │  │  Azure SQL      │     │","│  │  (Node 20)      │  │  (Azure CNI)    │  │  (Basic SKU)    │     │","│  │                 │  │                 │  │                 │     │","│  │  snet-web       │  │  snet-aks       │  │  snet-data      │     │","│  │  10.1.1.0/24    │  │  10.1.2.0/23    │  │  10.1.4.0/24    │     │","│  │  🛡 nsg-web     │  │  🛡 nsg-aks     │  │  🛡 nsg-data    │     │","│  └────────┬────────┘  └───────┬─────────┘  └───────┬─────────┘     │","│           │    HTTPS :443     │    SQL :1433        │               │","│    Internet ─────────────────▶├────────────────────▶│               │","└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘","```","","**Traffic flow:** Users hit the App Service frontend over HTTPS. The frontend calls the AKS-hosted API. The API queries Azure SQL. Each hop is restricted by NSG rules — no tier can be reached by anything other than its intended upstream.","","---","","## Design decisions","","### Why Hub-and-Spoke?","","The job description mentions Hub-and-Spoke as part of the platform architecture at TJIP. This pattern separates shared infrastructure (firewall, VPN gateways, DNS) in the Hub from workload resources in the Spoke. It is the standard approach in Azure landing zones and makes it easy to add more spokes (e.g. a staging spoke, a production spoke) without touching shared services.","","### Why AKS for the application tier?","","AKS is listed as a core part of TJIP's tech stack. Using it here, instead of a second App Service, shows how the API tier would work in practice. I chose **Azure CNI** for networking because it assigns pod IPs directly from the AKS subnet, which means NSG rules and VNet peering work natively without overlay networks. The `/23` subnet gives AKS enough IP space to scale.","","### Why App Service for the web tier?","","A simple frontend does not need container orchestration. App Service is fully managed, supports VNet integration, and keeps the presentation tier lightweight. This also shows I can pick the right service for the job rather than using AKS for everything.","","Instead of deploying custom application code, the frontend runs **Microsoft's official sample container** (`mcr.microsoft.com/appsvc/staticsite:latest`). This is a public image from the Microsoft Container Registry designed exactly for infrastructure demos — it gives you a working web page that confirms the App Service is running correctly. In a real project, this would be swapped for the team's frontend container or code via CI/CD.","","### Why Azure SQL with VNet rules?","","Azure SQL is a managed relational database — no patching, no backups to manage. I locked it down with `public_network_access_enabled = false` and a VNet service endpoint rule so only the data subnet can reach it. In production I would use a Private Endpoint instead (more secure, but more complex for a demo).","","### Security \u0026 compliance thinking","","Even though this is a small demo, I made choices that reflect an ISO27001/SOC2-aware mindset:","","- **System-assigned Managed Identity** on AKS — avoids storing service principal secrets.","- **NSG deny-all rules** on the app and data subnets — explicit deny at the bottom of the rule list.","- **SQL password as a sensitive variable**, Terraform will not show it in plan output.","- **Public access disabled** on the SQL server.","- **Consistent tagging** — every resource gets `Project`, `Environment`, and `ManagedBy` tags for audit trails.","","### What I intentionally left out","","These are things I would add in a real platform but excluded to keep the assignment focused:","","| Excluded | Why it matters in production |","|----------|------------------------------|","| Azure Firewall resource | The Hub subnet is ready for it, but the firewall SKU is expensive for a demo |","| Ingress controller (NGINX / App Gateway) | Needed to route external traffic into AKS pods |","| Azure Monitor + Grafana | TJIP's observability stack — out of scope per the assignment |","| Azure DevOps CI/CD pipelines | Out of scope per the assignment |","| Terragrunt wrapper | Would use in production for DRY config across environments |","| Remote state backend | Would use Azure Storage Account with blob lease locking |","| Key Vault for secrets | SQL password would live here instead of in a variable |","| Private Endpoints | More secure than VNet rules, but adds complexity |","| Pod-level network policies | Calico or Azure NPM for intra-cluster traffic control |","","---","","## Assumptions","","1. You have the **Azure CLI** installed and are logged in (`az login`).","2. You have **Terraform \u003e= 1.5** (or OpenTofu) installed.","3. You have an Azure subscription with permissions to create resources.","4. The **West Europe** region is acceptable (closest to the Delft office).","5. This is a dev/demo environment — production would need the items listed above.","","---","","## How to run it","","### 1. Enter the project directory","","```bash","cd terraform-3tier","```","","### 2. Create your variable file","","```bash","cp terraform.tfvars.example terraform.tfvars","# Edit terraform.tfvars — at minimum set a strong sql_admin_password","```","","### 3. Initialize Terraform","","```bash","terraform init","```","","Downloads the AzureRM provider plugin.","","### 4. Preview the plan","","```bash","terraform plan","```","","Review the output — you should see around 20 resources to be created.","","### 5. Apply (optional — creates real Azure resources and incurs costs)","","```bash","terraform apply","# Type \"yes\" when prompted","```","","### 6. Connect to AKS (after apply)","","```bash","az aks get-credentials \\","  --resource-group rg-threetier-dev \\","  --name aks-threetier-dev","","kubectl get nodes","```","","### 7. Tear down","","```bash","terraform destroy","```","","---","","## Project structure","","```","terraform-3tier/","├── main.tf                  # Provider config, resource group","├── variables.tf             # All input variables with validation","├── locals.tf                # Shared tags","├── network.tf               # Hub VNet, Spoke VNet, peering, subnets, NSGs","├── web.tf                   # Tier 1 — App Service (frontend)","├── aks.tf                   # Tier 2 — AKS cluster (API)","├── database.tf              # Tier 3 — Azure SQL Server + database","├── outputs.tf               # Useful output values","├── terraform.tfvars.example # Example variable values","└── README.md                # This file","```","","---","","## Notes for the follow-up discussion","","Things I am happy to walk through in person:","","- **Why Hub-and-Spoke over a flat VNet** — and how you would add a second spoke for staging/prod.","- **Azure CNI vs Kubenet** — trade-offs around IP consumption, NSG compatibility, and performance.","- **How Terragrunt would wrap this** — using `terragrunt.hcl` files per environment to keep the Terraform DRY.","- **Landing zone evolution** — how this small project would grow into a full platform with Azure Policy, management groups, and subscription-level isolation.","- **Compliance controls** — how tagging, managed identities, and network isolation map to ISO27001/SOC2 controls."],"stylingDirectives":null,"colorizedLines":["\u003cspan class=\"pl-mh\"\u003e# \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eAzure 3-Tier Application Infrastructure\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e","","A Terraform project that defines infrastructure for a 3-tier web application on Microsoft Azure, using a \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003eHub-and-Spoke network topology\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e — the same pattern used in landing zones for financial-sector platforms.","","No application code is deployed. This is purely infrastructure-as-code.","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-ms\"\u003e---\u003c/span\u003e","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-mh\"\u003e## \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eArchitecture overview\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e```\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                    ┌──────────────────────────────────────┐\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                    │        Hub VNet  10.0.0.0/16         │\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                    │                                      │\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                    │   ┌──────────────────────────────┐   │\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                    │   │  AzureFirewallSubnet          │   │\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                    │   │  10.0.1.0/24                  │   │\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                    │   │  (central egress \u0026amp; logging)   │   │\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                    │   └──────────────────────────────┘   │\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                    └──────────────┬───────────────────────┘\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                                   │\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                              VNet Peering\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                                   │\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e┌──────────────────────────────────┴───────────────────────────────────┐\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e│                     Spoke VNet  10.1.0.0/16                         │\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e│                                                                     │\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e│  ┌─────────────────┐  ┌─────────────────┐  ┌─────────────────┐     │\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e│  │  TIER 1 · WEB   │  │  TIER 2 · APP   │  │  TIER 3 · DATA  │     │\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e│  │                 │  │                 │  │                 │     │\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e│  │  App Service    │  │  AKS Cluster    │  │  Azure SQL      │     │\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e│  │  (Node 20)      │  │  (Azure CNI)    │  │  (Basic SKU)    │     │\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e│  │                 │  │                 │  │                 │     │\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e│  │  snet-web       │  │  snet-aks       │  │  snet-data      │     │\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e│  │  10.1.1.0/24    │  │  10.1.2.0/23    │  │  10.1.4.0/24    │     │\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e│  │  🛡 nsg-web     │  │  🛡 nsg-aks     │  │  🛡 nsg-data    │     │\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e│  └────────┬────────┘  └───────┬─────────┘  └───────┬─────────┘     │\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e│           │    HTTPS :443     │    SQL :1433        │               │\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e│    Internet ─────────────────▶├────────────────────▶│               │\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e```\u003c/span\u003e","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003eTraffic flow:\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e Users hit the App Service frontend over HTTPS. The frontend calls the AKS-hosted API. The API queries Azure SQL. Each hop is restricted by NSG rules — no tier can be reached by anything other than its intended upstream.","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-ms\"\u003e---\u003c/span\u003e","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-mh\"\u003e## \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eDesign decisions\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-mh\"\u003e### \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eWhy Hub-and-Spoke?\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e","","The job description mentions Hub-and-Spoke as part of the platform architecture at TJIP. This pattern separates shared infrastructure (firewall, VPN gateways, DNS) in the Hub from workload resources in the Spoke. It is the standard approach in Azure landing zones and makes it easy to add more spokes (e.g. a staging spoke, a production spoke) without touching shared services.","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-mh\"\u003e### \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eWhy AKS for the application tier?\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e","","AKS is listed as a core part of TJIP\u0026#39;s tech stack. Using it here — instead of a second App Service — shows how the API tier would work in practice. I chose \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003eAzure CNI\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e for networking because it assigns pod IPs directly from the AKS subnet, which means NSG rules and VNet peering work natively without overlay networks. The \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e/23\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e subnet gives AKS enough IP space to scale.","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-mh\"\u003e### \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eWhy App Service for the web tier?\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e","","A simple frontend does not need container orchestration. App Service is fully managed, supports VNet integration, and keeps the presentation tier lightweight. This also shows I can pick the right service for the job rather than using AKS for everything.","","Instead of deploying custom application code, the frontend runs \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003eMicrosoft\u0026#39;s official sample container\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e (\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003emcr.microsoft.com/appsvc/staticsite:latest\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e). This is a public image from the Microsoft Container Registry designed exactly for infrastructure demos, it gives you a working web page that confirms the App Service is running correctly. In a real project, this would be swapped for the team\u0026#39;s frontend container or code via CI/CD.","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-mh\"\u003e### \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eWhy Azure SQL with VNet rules?\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e","","Azure SQL is a managed relational database — no patching, no backups to manage. I locked it down with \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003epublic_network_access_enabled = false\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e and a VNet service endpoint rule so only the data subnet can reach it. In production I would use a Private Endpoint instead (more secure, but more complex for a demo).","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-mh\"\u003e### \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eSecurity \u0026amp; compliance thinking\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e","","Even though this is a small demo, I made choices that reflect an ISO27001/SOC2-aware mindset:","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003e-\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003eSystem-assigned Managed Identity\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e on AKS — avoids storing service principal secrets.","\u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003e-\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003eNSG deny-all rules\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e on the app and data subnets — explicit deny at the bottom of the rule list.","\u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003e-\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003eSQL password as a sensitive variable\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e — Terraform will not show it in plan output.","\u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003e-\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003ePublic access disabled\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e on the SQL server.","\u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003e-\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003eConsistent tagging\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e — every resource gets \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eProject\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eEnvironment\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e, and \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eManagedBy\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e tags for audit trails.","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-mh\"\u003e### \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eWhat I intentionally left out\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e","","These are things I would add in a real platform but excluded to keep the assignment focused:","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e Excluded \u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e Why it matters in production \u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e----------\u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e------------------------------\u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e Azure Firewall resource \u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e The Hub subnet is ready for it, but the firewall SKU is expensive for a demo \u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e Ingress controller (NGINX / App Gateway) \u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e Needed to route external traffic into AKS pods \u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e Azure Monitor + Grafana \u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e TJIP\u0026#39;s observability stack — out of scope per the assignment \u003cspan assignment \u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e Terragrunt wrapper \u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e Would use in production for DRY config across environments \u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e Remote state backend \u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e Would use Azure Storage Account with blob lease locking \u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e Key Vault for secrets \u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e SQL password would live here instead of in a variable \u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e Private Endpoints \u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e More secure than VNet rules, but adds complexity \u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e","\u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e Pod-level network policies \u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e Calico or Azure NPM for intra-cluster traffic control \u003cspan class=\"pl-ml\"\u003e|\u003c/span\u003e","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-ms\"\u003e---\u003c/span\u003e","","\u003cspan class=\"pl-mh\"\u003e## \u003cspan aria-labelledby="file-name-id-wide file-name-id-mobile" class="BlobContent-module__blobContentSection__VOgZq BlobContent-module__blobContentSectionMarkdown__mPLOK" style="margin-top:46px"><div class="Box-sc-62in7e-0 js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned BlobContent-module__markdownBlob__T8jpG" data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Azure 3-Tier Application Infrastructure</h1><a id="user-content-azure-3-tier-application-infrastructure" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Azure 3-Tier Application Infrastructure" href="#azure-3-tier-application-infrastructure"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A Terraform project that defines infrastructure for a 3-tier web application on Microsoft Azure, using a <strong>Hub-and-Spoke network topology</strong> , the same pattern used in landing zones for financial-sector platforms.</p>
<p dir="auto">No application code is deployed. This is purely infrastructure-as-code.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Architecture overview</h2><a id="user-content-architecture-overview" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Architecture overview" href="#architecture-overview"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="                    ┌──────────────────────────────────────┐

└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

<p dir="auto"><strong>Traffic flow:</strong> Users hit the App Service frontend over HTTPS. The frontend calls the AKS-hosted API. The API queries Azure SQL. Each hop is restricted by NSG rules; no tier can be reached by anything other than its intended upstream.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Design decisions</h2><a id="user-content-design-decisions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Design decisions" href="#design-decisions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Why Hub-and-Spoke?</h3><a id="user-content-why-hub-and-spoke" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Why Hub-and-Spoke?" href="#why-hub-and-spoke"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The challenge description mentions Hub-and-Spoke as part of the platform architecture at TJIP. This pattern separates shared infrastructure (firewall, VPN gateways, DNS) in the Hub from workload resources in the Spoke. It is the standard approach in Azure landing zones and makes it easy to add more spokes (e.g. a staging spoke, a production spoke) without touching shared services.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Why AKS for the application tier?</h3><a id="user-content-why-aks-for-the-application-tier" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Why AKS for the application tier?" href="#why-aks-for-the-application-tier"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">AKS is listed as a core part of TJIP's tech stack. Using it here — instead of a second App Service — shows how the API tier would work in practice. I chose <strong>Azure CNI</strong> for networking because it assigns pod IPs directly from the AKS subnet, which means NSG rules and VNet peering work natively without overlay networks. The <code>/23</code> subnet gives AKS enough IP space to scale.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Why App Service for the web tier?</h3><a id="user-content-why-app-service-for-the-web-tier" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Why App Service for the web tier?" href="#why-app-service-for-the-web-tier"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A simple frontend does not need container orchestration. App Service is fully managed, supports VNet integration, and keeps the presentation tier lightweight. This also shows I can pick the right service for the job rather than using AKS for everything.</p>
<p dir="auto">Instead of deploying custom application code, the frontend runs <strong>Microsoft's official sample container</strong> (<code>mcr.microsoft.com/appsvc/staticsite:latest</code>). This is a public image from the Microsoft Container Registry designed exactly for infrastructure demos — it gives you a working web page that confirms the App Service is running correctly. In a real project, this would be swapped for the team's frontend container or code via CI/CD.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Why Azure SQL with VNet rules?</h3><a id="user-content-why-azure-sql-with-vnet-rules" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Why Azure SQL with VNet rules?" href="#why-azure-sql-with-vnet-rules"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Azure SQL is a managed relational database, no patching, no backups to manage. I locked it down with <code>public_network_access_enabled = false</code> and a VNet service endpoint rule so only the data subnet can reach it. In production I would use a Private Endpoint instead (more secure, but more complex for a demo).</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Security &amp; compliance thinking</h3><a id="user-content-security--compliance-thinking" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Security &amp; compliance thinking" href="#security--compliance-thinking"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Even though this is a small demo, I made choices that reflect an ISO27001/SOC2-aware mindset:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>System-assigned Managed Identity</strong> on AKS — avoids storing service principal secrets.</li>
<li><strong>NSG deny-all rules</strong> on the app and data subnets — explicit deny at the bottom of the rule list.</li>
<li><strong>SQL password as a sensitive variable</strong> — Terraform will not show it in plan output.</li>
<li><strong>Public access disabled</strong> on the SQL server.</li>
<li><strong>Consistent tagging</strong>: every resource gets <code>Project</code>, <code>Environment</code>, and <code>ManagedBy</code> tags for audit trails.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">What I intentionally left out</h3><a id="user-content-what-i-intentionally-left-out" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: What I intentionally left out" href="#what-i-intentionally-left-out"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">These are things I would add in a real platform but excluded to keep the assignment focused:</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Excluded</th>
<th>Why it matters in production</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Azure Firewall resource</td>
<td>The Hub subnet is ready for it, but the firewall SKU is expensive for a demo</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Ingress controller (NGINX / App Gateway)</td>
<td>Needed to route external traffic into AKS pods</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Azure Monitor + Grafana</td>
<td>TJIP's observability stack — out of scope per the assignment</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Azure DevOps CI/CD pipelines</td>
<td>Out of scope per the assignment</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Terragrunt wrapper</td>
<td>Would use in production for DRY config across environments</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Remote state backend</td>
<td>Would use Azure Storage Account with blob lease locking</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Key Vault for secrets</td>
<td>SQL password would live here instead of in a variable</td>
</tr>

<td>More secure than VNet rules, but adds complexity</td>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Assumptions</h2><a id="user-content-assumptions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Assumptions" href="#assumptions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>You have the <strong>Azure CLI</strong> installed and are logged in (<code>az login</code>).</li>
<li>You have <strong>Terraform &gt;= 1.5</strong> (or OpenTofu) installed.</li>
<li>You have an Azure subscription with permissions to create resources.</li>
<li>The <strong>West Europe</strong> region is acceptable (closest to the Delft office).</li>
<li>This is a dev/demo environment — production would need the items listed above.</li>
</ol>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">How to run it</h2><a id="user-content-how-to-run-it" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How to run it" href="#how-to-run-it"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">1. <div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="terraform init"><pre>terraform init</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Downloads the AzureRM provider plugin.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">4. Preview the plan</h3><a id="user-content-4-preview-the-plan" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 4. Preview the plan" href="#4-preview-the-plan"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="terraform plan"><pre>terraform plan</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Review the output — you should see around 20 resources to be created.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5. Apply (optional — creates real Azure resources and incurs costs)</h3><a id="user-content-5-apply-optional--creates-real-azure-resources-and-incurs-costs" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5. Apply (optional — creates real Azure resources and incurs costs)" href="#5-apply-optional--creates-real-azure-resources-and-incurs-costs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="terraform apply

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Notes for the follow-up discussion</h2><a id="user-content-notes-for-the-follow-up-discussion" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Notes for the follow-up discussion" href="#notes-for-the-follow-up-discussion"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Things I am happy to walk through in person:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Why Hub-and-Spoke over a flat VNet</strong> — and how you would add a second spoke for staging/prod.</li>
<li><strong>Azure CNI vs Kubenet</strong> — trade-offs around IP consumption, NSG compatibility, and performance.</li>
<li><strong>How Terragrunt would wrap this</strong> — using <code>terragrunt.hcl</code> files per environment to keep the Terraform DRY.</li>
<li><strong>Landing zone evolution</strong> — how this small project would grow into a full platform with Azure Policy, management groups, and subscription-level isolation.</li>
<li><strong>Compliance controls</strong> — how tagging, managed identities, and network isolation map to ISO27001/SOC2 controls.</li>
</ul>
